		<script>
			$(function(){
				var fetchCategory = function(val){
					$.post("https://caripromo.id/cari", { ac: 'category', category: val }, function(resp){
						$('.category').html(resp);
					});
				}
				fetchCategory("");
				$('.filterCategory').keyup(function(e){
					var code = e.keyCode || e.which;
					var _val = $(this).val();
					if(_val && code != 13) fetchCategory(_val);
				});
			});
